Was happy to find this local business! I visited this cute cupcake shop today to get cupcakes as a birthday gift, and pick up a couple extra while I was there. I tried the lemon blueberry, and that's what made me write this review. OMG so good! A lemon cupcake and with blueberry frosting, right? No. It has a surprising layer of tart but sweet (but pretty tart!) lemon glaze in between the sweet, but not too sweet, blueberry frosting.and cupcake. Delicious! Will be going back for sure.</text>

The gluten free cupcake was chocolate with a raspberry frosting. Normally I would not enjoy chocolate with berry, but this was an Awesome cupcake- it was moist and soft, and tasted more like a brownie, and the frosting was a deep rich flavor. It was so rich I actually had to eat it in two separate sittings. My daughter enjoyed the cake pop. The was also a pumpkin cookie available gluten free.
The atmosphere was eclectic and fun almost like Alice in wonderland. Whimsical and creativity inspiring. It was an enjoyable visit.</Review>

< text>
------------------------
UPDATE 8/29/17:
Arrived again on 8/12/17 for our Camarones a la Diabla. 5 guys ordered it and all 5 pronounced it as the best they have eaten yet anywhere. Don't know what other reviewers are eating but make no mistake - there is NOTHING bland about the Camarones and it IS authentic. Try it and let me know what you think. Or, don't and we'll have more for us, lol!
------------------------------------------

We have been using this establishment for going on 15 years now. It is a lunch destination spot for our little motorcycle group, and we go for one thing and one thing only - Camarones a la Diabla. It is consistently the best we've ever found + they own the tortilla factory next store so those are fresh as can be as well. Sublime heat and flavor combo. Somebody said this place was flavorless? LOL! But don't listen to me, go taste for yourself. I'm headed there tomorrow and can't wait, maybe I'll see you there.
PS: They appear to be open Sundays now but I also hear that they close one Sunday a month so take note.< /text>

< Review>
Had to see what the fuss has been about their spicy chicken sandwich. I've tested spicy chicken sandwiches everywhere and  it ranks in the top three of the major food chains. The portion is large. The pickles are fresh and crispy, not sour. The hot sauce in the sandwich on its own was pleasant, but with a serving of their side hot sauce, it was popping. I believe others have given this original spicy chicken sandwich a run for its money, but it still stands.< /Review>

< review>
Just off China town, this is a great place for vegans, vegetarians and curious omnivores. If you want to show your omnivore friends how meat substitutes taste like, this is the place.
We tried the pork, chicken and beef meals on 2 different occasions, the beef and chicken were very tasty. Beef with daikon and chicken with basil are personal favourites.

The place is quiet, food comes fast, no queues. Service might be a tad forgetful but in general friendly.

Definitely worth a visit!</review>

<text>5 stars for the best Tri-Tip I have ever had. Not even Dog House Gill or Mike's Grill (both in Fresno) can beat it. I will come back and would be willing to drive from Fresno just to get some. The place is tiny so it looks a bit messy and there is almost no room to wait for your food, but since you can only pick-up it doesn't matter to me. I saw the cook outside and could smell the goodness as I approached from afar. Oh and the Mac and Cheese was uniquely amazing. Service was relatively quick specially since I called in my order, but I'm big on customer service so I would say they need to up there game and be a bit more relational with casual conversation  instead of just the "hi and bye" additude . Don't get me wrong, they seem really nice and they did wish me a good lunch but that was one thing I saw could use improvement, oh and maybe hire at least one other person because I only saw 2 people working. I would totally recommend this to anyone that loves meat! Hope this was helpful and I hope you enjoy it if you try it.< /text>< resp>

Three years ago I became interested in purchasing gold and silver bullion, largely as a hedge against inflation.  My only previous exposure was gold stock.  I actually made my first "bullion" purchases on three different internet sites. They all turned out to be fake silver eagles. Beautiful -but fake. Disreputable sellers are out there, with attractive pricing and merchandise waiting to take advantage of you.

I then learned how to tell  fake coins from real coins.  One has to know what to look for - but the tells are obvious. I even constructed a "silver coin slide"  tool made with high power magnets I purchased on "Amazon. The slide test results are amazing and definitive. The attached photo shows a beautiful fake silver eagle firmly stuck on my slide tool.

My lesson and advice is to only buy from a reliable seller.

Advantage Gold is such a reliable seller.

I have since bought both gold and silver bullion from Advantage Gold.
George Bush  of Advantage Gold made my first purchase simple and efficient. I used, and recommend  bank transfers.  My actual time at the bank is measured in minutes. My bullion arrived promptly and securely at my door and now resides at the bank.< /text>

<Text>I worked with Travis Griffin for almost two years before finally investing some of my IRA money in gold and silver. My hesitance was the result of the incessant marketing of gold and silver on TV and the Internet. I was also cautious because I am semi-retired and therefore already withdrawing some of my retirement assets to pay for our living expenses.

I never experienced the "hard sell" approach from Travis and Advantage Gold that led to my reticence. Their main goal was to educate me in the way that gold would fit in with my investment objectives. As a financial advisor, I am used to more traditional investment vehicles, but the information provided by Travis and Advantage convinced me that there was a place for precious metals in my portfolio.

I heartily recommend Advantage Gold to anyone interested in investing in precious metals.< /Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< Response>
